class="qtR3Y" data-hveid="82"><span class="Y0NH2b CLPzrc g9yevd">A probability of <b>precipitation</b> or POP of 40% doesn't <b>mean</b> that it will rain 40% of the day, or that rain will fall on 40% It also says nothing about how much rain or snow will occur.</span></div><!--n--></div><div class="g"><!--m--><div data-hveid="84" data-ved="0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8QFQhUKAAwCA"><div class="rc"><h3 class="r"><a href="http://www.islandnet.com/~see/weather/whys/pop.htm" onmousedown="return rwt(this,'','','','9','AOvVaw3lMnURhiuFbVVobILVnMCd','','0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8QFghVMAg','','',event)">The Weather Doctor: Weather Whys - Islandnet.com</a></h3><div class="s"><div><div class="f hJND5c TbwUpd" style="white-space:nowrap"><cite class="iUh30">www.islandnet.com/~see/weather/whys/pop.htm</cite></div></div></div></div></div><!--n--></div><div class="BrAQvb match-mod-horizontal-padding">Search for: <a data-original-name="What does it mean 100% rain?" href="/search?q=What+does+it+mean+100%25+rain%3F&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8QzmcIVg" data-ved="0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8QzmcIVg">What does it mean 100% rain?</a></div></div></div></div></div><div decode-data-ved="1" eid="AYqxWpW-MYnvzgKfy7v4DA" class="iUzEaCqUiVTc-q0_7ulvsJF4 m7VU0c related-question-pair r-irGyDyq9XxSU" jsaction="dummy:r.J9jIHVdh6Uw" data-rtid="irGyDyq9XxSU" jsl="$t t-q3HL14F6HpU;$x 0;" data-ved="0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8Qq7kBCFcoAw"><div class="s30t1e match-mod-horizontal-padding nmiw nmtbi nmt irGyDyq9XxSU-Dxg0p2iqJnc" aria-expanded="false" role="button" tabindex="0" jsaction="r.J9jIHVdh6Uw" data-rtid="irGyDyq9XxSU" jsl="$x 0;" data-hveid="88" data-ved="0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8Quk4IWCgA"><div class="fYWO0d"></div><div class="psDd8d"><div class="NWt7k">What does it mean when there is a 70% chance of rain?</div></div></div><div class="nmcw nmbl irGyDyq9XxSU-GQSfLE1fUrA" data-hveid="89" data-ved="0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8Qu04IWSgB"><div id="irq9"><div class="KJ2SMb"><div class="mod" data-md="61" style="clear:none"><!--m--><div class="qtR3Y" data-hveid="90"><span class="Y0NH2b CLPzrc g9yevd">Strictly speaking, a <b>70</b>% <b>chance of rain means</b> that there is a <b>70</b>% <b>chance</b> of measurable precipitation (0.01 inch or more) at a specific area in a twelve-hour period. This figure would be used if there's a <b>70</b>% <b>chance of rain</b> over 100% of the area, or if <b>rain</b> is certain (a 100% <b>chance</b>) over <b>70</b>% of the area.</span></div><!--n--></div><div class="g"><!--m--><div data-hveid="92" data-ved="0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8QFQhcKAAwCg"><div class="rc"><h3 class="r"><a href="http://www.wxdude.com/mostasked.html" onmousedown="return rwt(this,'','','','11','AOvVaw1mxvkIaBZdqGn4YneZSgKP','','0ahUKEwjVwsjA-PvZAhWJt1MKHZ_lDs8QFghdMAo','','',event)">Most Asked Weather Questions -
